<div>   
<table><tbody><tr><td width="50%"> Clustering on mixed type data </td><td> 对混乱的数据进行聚类 </td></tr><tr><td> <section><h1>Clustering on mixed type data</h1><h2>A proposed approach using R</h2><h4>ABOUT</h4><p>Clustering <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unsupervised_learning">unsupervised data</a> is not an easy task. Indeed, data crunching and exploration is in such a context often driven by domain knowledge, if not pure intuition, and made difficult as there is no way to measure the accuracy of the resulting segmentation (as opposed to supervised learning).</p><p>In addition, introductory courses to unsupervised learning quite often discuss ideal use cases, such as k-means tutorials, which only apply to numerical features.</p><p>However, real business situations often deviate from these ideal use cases, and need to analyze datasets made of mixed-type data, where numeric (the difference between two values is meaningful), nominal(categorical, not ordered) or ordinal (categorical, ordered) features coexist.</p><p>In this post, I’m focusing on such situations, in the context of unsupervised classification exercise using R.</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>The first part covers methodology: I’m discussing the issue of measuring similarity across individuals, using the mathematical concept of distance. I then introduce the PAM clustering algorithm (partitioning around medoids) as well as a way to select optimal number of clusters(silhouette coefficient). I lastly close with a word on interpretation.</p></li><li><p>In the second part, I’m illustrating the approach using a bank marketing dataset available on uci's <a href="https://archive.ics.uci.edu/ml/datasets/Bank+Marketing">machine learning repository</a>, and some useful functions from <code>cluster</code> and <code>Rtsne</code> packages. This dataset is related with direct marketing campaigns (phone calls) of a Portuguese banking institution and is traditionally used for supervised learning disussion (the classification goal is to predict if the client will subscribe a term deposit). However it contains some information about bank clients, which we will try to cluster ‘a priori’.</p></li></ul><p>Let’s get started!</p></section><p><br></p><section> </section></td><td> <p><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml><w:LatentStyles DefLockedState="false"  DefUnhideWhenUsed="true"  DefSemiHidden="true"  DefQFormat="false"  DefPriority="99"  LatentStyleCount="260" >

</td></tr><tr><td> <h3>PART I: METHODOLOGY</h3><h4>HOW TO MEASURE SIMILARITY</h4><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230187124455.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p><p>Data Scientists aiming at clustering ‘unknown’ data, sometimes without business knowledge, use distance to avoid subjectivity and ensure consistent approach to all features</p><p>Distance is a numerical measurement of how far apart individuals are, i.e. a metrics used to measure proximity or similarity across individuals. Many distance metrics exist, and one is actually quite useful to crack our case, the Gower distance (1971).</p> </td><td> <p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;" style="font-size: xx-large; font-weight: bold;"><font face="宋体">第一部分：方法论</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml><w:LatentStyles DefLockedState="false"  DefUnhideWhenUsed="true"  DefSemiHidden="true"  DefQFormat="false"  DefPriority="99"  LatentStyleCount="260" >

div.Section0&#123;page:Section0;&#125;</style></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">对未知数据进行聚类的数据科学家有时不考虑商业知识而直接使用距离来避免主观性，并确保对所有特征采用相同的方法。距离是一种对个体相差多远的数值化测量方法，即用于测量个体间的接近度或相似度的指标。存在许多距离度量，其中之一实际上非常有助于破解我们的情况，</font>Gower<font face="宋体">距离（</font><font face="Calibri">1971</font><font face="宋体">）。有很多的距离度量方法，其中一个十分有助于解决我们这个问题的就是，</font><font face="Calibri">Gower</font><font face="宋体">距离（</font><font face="Calibri">1971</font><font face="宋体">）。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><br></p> </td></tr><tr><td> <p>Gower distance is computed as the average of partial dissimilarities across individuals. Each partial dissimilarity (and thus Gower distance) ranges in [0 1].</p><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230186831355.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p><p>Gower distance’s formula</p><p>Partial dissimilarities (<code>d_ij^f</code>) computation depend on the type of variable being evaluated. This implies that a particular standardization will be applied to each feature, and the distance between two individuals is the average of all feature-specific distances.</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>For a numerical feature <code>f</code>, partial dissimilarity is the ratio between 1) absolute difference of observations <code>x_i</code> and <code>x_j</code>and 2) maximum range observed from all individuals: <code>d_ij^f = |x_i — x_j| / |(max_N(x) — min_N(x))|</code> , N being the number of individuals in the dataset.</p></li></ul><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230186138747.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p><p>Partial dissimilarity computation for numerical features (R_f = maximal range observed)</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>For a qualitative feature <code>f</code> partial dissimilarity equals 1 only if observations <code>y_i</code> and <code>y_j</code> have different value. Zero otherwise.</p></li></ul><p>Note: Gower distance is available in R using <code>daisy()</code>function from the <code>cluster </code>package. Features are first automatically standardized (i.e. rescaled to fall in a [0 1] range).</p> </td><td> <p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">高尔距离计算公式如上。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">局部相似度</font>d_ij^f <font face="宋体">的计算取决于要估计的变量类型。这意味着在每个特征上都会被加上一种特殊的标准化方式，且两个独立样本间的高尔距离既是所有具体特征的平均距离。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">  -<font face="宋体">对于数值特征</font><font face="Calibri">f</font><font face="宋体">，局部差异性是 观测值 </font><font face="Calibri">x_i </font><font face="宋体">与 </font><font face="Calibri">x_j</font><font face="宋体">做差的绝对值 与 所有独立样本中的最大观测范围</font><font face="Calibri">: d_if^f = |x_i - x_j | / |max_N(x) - min_N(y) | </font><font face="宋体">二者之比。 </font><font face="Calibri">N</font><font face="宋体">是 数据集中样本个数。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">局部差异性特征被用于计算数值特征</font>R<font face="宋体">（</font><font face="Calibri">R_f = </font><font face="宋体">最大观测值范围）</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">   -<font face="宋体">对于定性的特征</font><font face="Calibri">f</font><font face="宋体">，局部差异性只有在 </font><font face="Calibri">y_i </font><font face="宋体">与 </font><font face="Calibri">y_j </font><font face="宋体">在观测值上不同时等于</font><font face="Calibri">1</font><font face="宋体">，否则等于</font><font face="Calibri">0 </font><font face="宋体">。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p><!--[if gte roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">  <font face="宋体">小提示：如果你使用</font>R<font face="宋体">语言编程，可以在从</font><font face="Calibri">cluster</font><font face="宋体">包中的</font><font face="Calibri">daisy</font><font face="宋体">函数计算高尔距离。在使用前，特征会自动标准化（被规范到</font><font face="Calibri">0:1</font><font face="宋体">）</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><br clear="all"></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p> </td></tr><tr><td> <h4>CLUSTERING ALGORITHM: PARTITIONING AROUND MEDOIDS (PAM)<br></h4><p>The Gower distance fits well with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K-medoids">k-medoids algorithm</a>. k-medoid is a classical partitioning technique of clustering that clusters the data set of n objects into k clusters known a priori.</p><p>Pretty similar to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K-means_clustering">k-means algorithm</a>, PAM has the following caracteristics:</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>Pros: it’s intuitive, more robust to noise and outliers compared to k-means (due to the properties of distances being used), and it produces a “typical individual” for each cluster (useful for interpretation).</p></li><li><p>Cons: it’s time consuming and computer intensive (run time and memory are quadratic).</p></li></ul> </td><td> <p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">聚类算法：</font>MEDOIDS<font face="宋体">分割</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">高尔距离在</font>k-medoids <font face="宋体">算法中得到了很好的应用。</font><font face="Calibri">K-medoids </font><font face="宋体">是一种经典的聚类算法。该算法主要用于将含有</font><font face="Calibri">n</font><font face="宋体">类样本的数据集 转化</font><font face="Calibri">k</font><font face="宋体">类样本的 聚类问题。其中</font><font face="Calibri">k</font><font face="宋体">作为先验知识已知。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">与</font>k-means<font face="宋体">算法相似，</font><font face="Calibri">PAM</font><font face="宋体">算法有以下特点：</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">   - <font face="宋体">优点： 从直觉上而言，</font><font face="Calibri">PAM</font><font face="宋体">相对于</font><font face="Calibri">k-means</font><font face="宋体">对于噪声与离群点数据有着更好的鲁棒性。（由于算法使用了特征距离），而且算法对于结果中的每个类别都对应一个“代表性样本”（用于对算法结果进行解释）</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p><!--[if div.Section0&#123;page:Section0;&#125;</style></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;">   - <font face="宋体">缺点：算法计算比较耗时并且本身是密集型计算。（时间与空间复杂度都是</font><font face="Calibri">n^2</font><font face="宋体">）</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p> </td></tr><tr><td> <h4>ASSESS CONSISTENCY WITHIN CLUSTERS OF DATA<br></h4><p>Unless you have a good a priori rationale to force a specific number of clusters k, you might be interested in asking the computer for a recommendation based on statistics. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cluster_analysis#Evaluation_and_assessment">Several approaches exist</a> to qualify the relevancy of chosen number of clusters. In part II, we use the silhouette coefficient.</p><p>The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Silhouette_%28clustering%29">silhouette coefficient</a> contrasts the average distance to elements in the same cluster with the average distance to elements in other clusters. Objects with a high silhouette value are considered well clustered, objects with a low value may be outliers. This index works well with k-medoids clustering, and is also used to determine the optimal number of clusters. Please read the Wikipedia page for further details around computation and interpretation.</p><h4>INTERPRETATION</h4><p>There are basically two ways to investigate the results of such a clustering exercise, in order to derive some business-relevant interpretation.</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>1. Summary of each cluster, using <code>summary()</code> function in R.</p></li><li><p>2. Visualization in a lower dimensional space, with <a href="https://lvdmaaten.github.io/tsne/">t-SNE</a>, using <code>Rtsne()</code> function in R. t-Distributed Stochastic Neighbor Embedding (t-SNE) is a technique for dimensionality reduction that is particularly well suited for the visualization of high-dimensional datasets.</p></li></ul><p>We cover both cases in the use case (Part II). Enough for the theory, let’s apply and illustrate!</p><section> </section></td><td> <h4><b><spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="黑体">评估数据组内的一致性</font></spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></b><b><spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></b></h4><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">除非你有一个很强的先验能够使你确定聚类类别</font>K<font face="宋体">，否则你可能更希望计算机通过一些统计学的方法来给你一些推荐。目前有一些算法可以限定选择聚类数目的相关性。在第二部分中，我们将使用轮廓系数法。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">在同一类别中的元素与在不同类别中的元素，其平均轮廓系数有着很大的差别。有着高轮廓系数的样本会更有可能被归到同一类别，低轮廓系数的样本可能会被归到类外。这种度量指标非常适用于</font>k-medoids<font face="宋体">，而且也被应用于确定最佳聚类个数。有关计算和解释的更多细节，请阅读维基百科网页。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p> </o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><h2><b><spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="黑体">解释说明</font></spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></b><b><spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-weight:bold;font-size:16.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:黑体;mso-ascii-font-family:arial;mso-hansi-font-family:arial;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></b></h2><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">为了给出一些业务相关的解释，对于聚类问题，有两种基本的评估方法：</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p><p new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">在</font>R<font face="宋体">中使用</font><font face="Calibri">summary() </font><font face="宋体">函数，统计每一类包含的样本。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new class="MsoNormal"><!--[if !supportLists]--><spantimes new new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">使用</font>Rtsne()<font face="宋体">函数在低维空间中做数据可视化。</font><font face="Calibri">t-</font><font face="宋体">分布随机邻居嵌入</font><font face="Calibri">(t-sne)</font><font face="宋体">是一种降维技术，特别适用于高维数据集的可视化。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new div.Section0&#123;page:Section0;&#125;</style></p><p class="MsoNormal"><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><font face="宋体">我们在用下面的例子中</font>(<font face="宋体">第二部分</font><font face="Calibri">)</font><font face="宋体">介绍了这两个方法。理论知识部分已经足够了，下面我们来加以应用和说明。</font><spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times new roman';font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:1.0000pt;"><o:p></o:p></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></spanyes';font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:'times></p> </td></tr><tr><td> <h3>PART II: USE CASE</h3><p>In this use case, we will try to cluster bank clients according to the following characteristics:</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>age (numeric)</p></li><li><p>type of job (categorical): ‘admin.’, ’blue collar’, ’entrepreneur’, ’housemaid’, ’management’, ’retired’, ’self-employed’, ’services’, ’student’, ’technician’, ’unemployed’, ’unknown’</p></li><li><p>marital status (categorical): ‘divorced’, ’married’, ’single’, ’unknown’</p></li><li><p>education (categorical): ‘primary’, ‘secondary’, ‘tertiary’, ‘unknown’</p></li><li><p>default: has credit in default? (categorical): ‘no’, ’yes’, ’unknown’</p></li><li><p>balance (numeric): average yearly balance, in euros</p></li><li><p>housing: has housing loan? (categorical): ‘no’, ’yes’, ’unknown’</p></li></ul><pre>#' Load useful packages
library(cluster)
library(dplyr)
library(ggplot2)
library(readr)
library(Rtsne)</pre><pre>#' Load data
df <- read_csv2("../data/001_unsupervised_mixed_types_data/bank.csv")</pre><p>Most similar and dissimilar clients according to Gower distance:</p><pre>#' Compute Gower distance
gower_dist <- daisy(df, metric = "gower")</pre><pre>gower_mat <- as.matrix(gower_dist)</pre><pre>#' Print most similar clients
df[which(gower_mat == min(gower_mat[gower_mat != min(gower_mat)]), arr.ind = TRUE)[1, ], ]</pre><pre># A tibble: 2 x 7
    age job        marital education default balance housing
  <int> <fct>      <fct>   <fct>     <fct>     <int> <fct>  
1    52 technician married secondary no          196 yes    
2    52 technician married secondary no          195 yes</pre><pre>#' Print most dissimilar clients
df[which(gower_mat == max(gower_mat[gower_mat != max(gower_mat)]), arr.ind = TRUE)[1, ], ]</pre><pre># A tibble: 2 x 7
    age job     marital  education default balance housing
  <int> <fct>   <fct>    <fct>     <fct>     <int> <fct>  
1    60 retired married  primary   no        71188 no     
2    26 admin.  divorced secondary yes          -3 yes</pre> </td><td> <p><ahelp_5" name="help_5"><divpara-item clr"><divitem-area item-en edroll"></divitem-area></divpara-item></ahelp_5"></p><h3>第II部分: 用例</h3><p><ahelp_5" name="help_5"><divpara-item clr"><divitem-area item-en edroll"></divitem-area></divpara-item></ahelp_5"></p><p>在该用例中，我们将尝试根据以下特征对银行客户进行集群： </p><ahelp_5" name="help_5"><divpara-item clr"><divitem-area item-en edroll"><ul><li><p>age（年龄） (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', 微软雅黑, 宋体, 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">数值的  </spanmicrosoft>)</p></li><li><p>type of job （工作类型 ）(

<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: 200; letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">分类的  </spanmicrosoft>): ‘admin.’（行政）, ’blue collar’（蓝领）, ’entrepreneur’（创业家）, ’housemaid’（家庭主妇）, ’management’（管理）, ’retired’（退休的）, ’self-employed’（自雇）, ’services’（服务业）, ’student’（学生）, ’technician’（技工）, ’unemployed’（失业）, ’unknown’（未知）</p></li><li><p>marital status（婚姻状况） (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: 200; letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">分类的  </spanmicrosoft>): ‘divorced’（离异）, ’married’（已婚）, ’single’（单身）, ’unknown’（未知）</p></li><li><p>education（教育） (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: 200; letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">分类的  </spanmicrosoft>): ‘primary’（小学）, ‘secondary’（初中）, ‘tertiary’（大学）, ‘unknown’（未知）</p></li><li><p>default（违约）: 信用卡是否违约? (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: 200; letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">分类的  </spanmicrosoft>): ‘no’（否）, ’yes’（是）, ’unknown’（未知）</p></li><li><p>balance（余额） (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', 微软雅黑, 宋体, 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">数值的  </spanmicrosoft>): 平均年余额（欧元）</p></li><li><p>housing（房屋状况）: 是否有房贷? (

<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: 200; letter-spacing: line-height: 16.80000114440918px; orphans: auto; text-align: left; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); display: inline !important; float: none;">分类的  </spanmicrosoft>): ‘no’（否）, ’yes’（是）, ’unknown’（未知）</p></li></ul><pre>#' Load useful packages
library(cluster)
library(dplyr)
library(ggplot2)
library(readr)
library(Rtsne)</pre><pre>#' Load data
df <- read_csv2("../data/001_unsupervised_mixed_types_data/bank.csv")</pre><p><spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 25.987503051757813px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(247, 248, 250); display: inline !important; float: none;">根据高尔距离得出的最相似和最不同的客户:  </spanmicrosoft><br></p><pre>#' Compute Gower distance
gower_dist <- daisy(df, metric = "gower")

gower_mat <- as.matrix(gower_dist)

#' Print most similar clients
df[which(gower_mat == min(gower_mat[gower_mat != min(gower_mat)]), arr.ind = TRUE)[1, ], ]</pre><pre># A tibble: 2 x 7
    age job        marital education default balance housing
  <int> <fct>      <fct>   <fct>     <fct>     <int> <fct>  
1    52 technician married secondary no          196 yes    
2    52 technician married secondary no          195 yes

#' Print most dissimilar clients
df[which(gower_mat == max(gower_mat[gower_mat != max(gower_mat)]), arr.ind = TRUE)[1, ], ]</pre><pre># A tibble: 2 x 7
    age job     marital  education default balance housing
  <int> <fct>   <fct>    <fct>     <fct>     <int> <fct>  
1    60 retired married  primary   no        71188 no     
2    26 admin.  divorced secondary yes          -3 yes</pre></divitem-area></divpara-item></ahelp_5"> </td></tr><tr><td> <p>In business situation, we usually search for a number of clusters both meaningful and easy to remember, i.e. 2 to 8 maximum. The silhouette figure helps us identify the best option(s).<br></p><pre>sil_width <- c(NA)
for(i in 2:8)&#123;  
  pam_fit <- pam(gower_dist, diss = TRUE, k = i)  
  sil_width[i] <- pam_fit$silinfo$avg.width  
&#125;</pre><pre>plot(1:10, sil_width,
     xlab = "Number of clusters",
     ylab = "Silhouette Width")
lines(1:10, sil_width)</pre><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230186719459.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p> </td><td> <p><spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 25.987503051757813px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(247, 248, 250);">在商业情况下，我们通常会搜索2到8个既有意义又容易记忆的集群。用<spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 25.987503051757813px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(247, 248, 250);">轮廓图形帮助我们识别最佳选项。  </spanmicrosoft></spanmicrosoft></p><pre>sil_width <- c(NA)
for(i in 2:8)&#123;  
  pam_fit <- pam(gower_dist, diss = TRUE, k = i)  
  sil_width[i] <- pam_fit$silinfo$avg.width  
&#125;
plot(1:10, sil_width,
     xlab = "Number of clusters",
     ylab = "Silhouette Width")
lines(1:10, sil_width)</pre><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230186719459.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 25.987503051757813px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(247, 248, 250);"><spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; font-size: 13.600001335144043px; font-style: normal; font-variant: font-weight: letter-spacing: line-height: 25.987503051757813px; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: widows: word-spacing: -webkit-text-stroke-width: background-color: rgb(247, 248, 250);"><ahelp_6" name="help_6"><divpara-item clr"><divitem-area item-en edroll"><br></divitem-area></divpara-item></ahelp_6"></spanmicrosoft></spanmicrosoft></p> </td></tr><tr><td> <p>7 clusters has the highest silhouette width. 5 is simpler and almost as good. Let’s pick k = 5<br></p><p>Interpretation</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>Summary of each cluster</p></li></ul><pre>k <- 5
pam_fit <- pam(gower_dist, diss = TRUE, k)
pam_results <- df %>%
  mutate(cluster = pam_fit$clustering) %>%
  group_by(cluster) %>%
  do(the_summary = summary(.))
pam_results$the_summary</pre><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230187394485.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p><p>Clusters’ scorcard</p><p>Here one can attempt to derive some common patterns for clients within a cluster. As an example, cluster 1 is made of “management x tertiary x no default x no housing” clients, cluster 2 is made of “blue-collar x secondary x no default x housing” clients, etc.</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>Visualization in a lower dimensional space</p></li></ul><pre>tsne_obj <- Rtsne(gower_dist, is_distance = TRUE)</pre><pre>tsne_data <- tsne_obj$Y %>%
  data.frame() %>%
  setNames(c("X", "Y")) %>%
  mutate(cluster = factor(pam_fit$clustering))</pre><pre>ggplot(aes(x = X, y = Y), data = tsne_data) +
  geom_point(aes(color = cluster))</pre><p><br></p><p><img src="https://static.leiphone.com/uploads/new/sns/article/201808/1534230186865310.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><p><br></p><p>Clients observed in a lower dimensional space</p><p>Although not perfect (especially cluster 3), colors are mostly located in similar areas, confirming the relevancy of the segmentation.</p><section> </section></td><td> <p><spanmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif; I thought it could be of added value to other data scientists, thus the sharing.</p><p>Several challenges remain however, including:</p><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2"><li><p>How to deal with massive datasets (cf memory intensiveness)?</p></li><li><p>One hot encoding might be a solution; what are the pros and cons of these two approaches?</p></li></ul><p>Please do not hesitate to comment and share your vision on how to tackle this challenge and improve this proposed methodology.</p><section> </section></td><td> <p><ahelp_8" name="help_8"><divpara-item clr"><divitem-area item-en edroll"></divitem-area></divpara-item></ahelp_8"></p><h4>结论</h4><p><pmicrosoft yahei', '\\5fae软雅黑', '\\5b8b体', 'malgun gothic', meiryo, sans-serif;
